RATING: 8
When I first saw this game I couldn't understand how it was so well received.  When I played it for the first time, the experience wasn't enjoyable, but I could instantly see the potential.

After purchasing it for myself and hauling it around during a family vacation, I'm addicted.  Great fun in a short amount of time.  The beauty is in the moments where you're saying, "Okay, the only thing that could screw over all of my plans and bets right now is if a Blue 2 die comes  out."  And then it does! Much cheering and laughing.  The game is many of those  moments.

My adoration of this game continues to climb the more random group of people I break it out to.  I've played it at all kinds of situations, with all types of gamers, and it's just good clean fun having a group of people all cheering and jeering as a die pops out of the bottom.

It's just too great when everyone is debating odds and then you look at that Blue Camel trailing in the very back by 7 spaces and say, "Wouldn't it be great if Blue rolled a 3 and landed on that Oasis which put him on Orange, and then Orange rolled a 3 and suddenly Blue is winning?  Then someone takes that insane longshot bid, AND IT HAPPENS!"

RATING: 8
First opened at a campsite outside Bath, the rain was hammering down outside our little DIY canvas shelter. Expectations from the faces around me were very apprehensive but after 2 rounds we were all into our camel gambling personas.

The best thing about this game is the random nature of the outcome. Throughout the entire game Orange trailed - no winning bets were placed on it aside from the last to finish bid... the last two rolls saw this rocky-esque tango'd hero jump onto a cluster of camels only to depart at the last second to win by a nose length.

Swearing, cajoling and huge amounts of laughter were had - the exact ingredients for a brilliant gaming night... we even forgot it was raining!

RATING: 7
Camel Up is a horse race gambling game (except with camels, duh) that turns the usual formula on its head. Players bet through the different legs of each race, trying to predict which camel will finish in the lead. The trick is that when two or more camels are on the same space, they stack. The last one to arrive goes on top of the pile, and in a twist, is considered to be the leader.

All of this is almost completely random, yet it is interesting because you can almost calculate the odds for any given bet...but not quite, due to that unique stacking mechanic. In the biggest twist of all, anytime a camel at a lower position in the stack moves, it carries the camels on top of it. This creates a myriad of possibilities in each move and makes the wagering a real puzzle.

Again, it's completely random but just predictable enough to give the illusion of consistency to the players. This drives the betting and makes every turn have an agonizing decision, that usually doesn't work out for you, no matter how well you play the odds.

It's silly...and absolutely brilliant.

RATING: 7
Simple game, gives me a bit of a party-game vibe to me. This game requires almost no rules explanation, so it's easy to get to the table with non-gamers. Heavy game lovers might find the gambling aspect that is the core value proposition of this game too random, as you have to take quite some risks based on sparse information. I can totally imagine people not liking that.

I however don't mind it too much. I like to get a bit silly with the game and don't take things to seriously. I prefer to play multiple rounds and tally the money gained and announce a winner after X number of games.

RATING: 8.5
I was surprised by this game. Overly simple to play betting game. Admittedly all dice controlled, yet it's still fun. I snatched up the expansion (super cup) because the more I played this game, the more I fell in love with it. No other game makes me LOVE gambling quite like this gem. My only minor complaint is that the rubber band on the dice pyramid breaks after awhile, but rubber bands are relatively easy to come by. Bet on the race, bet on the leg of the race (all camel dice rolled), move the race, fix a bet. It's all so simple and flows so perfectly.

Artwork- 9/10
Theme- 7/10
Mechanics- 8/10
Fun- 8/10
